    <value>&lt;div align="justify"&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;Have you chosen attracting clients though your own website? InstaForex
    would like to give additional support to its customers by providing content and
    hosting for their websites absolutely for free! The only thing a client has to do
    is to purchase a domain name. Below, you will find out our recommendations for buying
    the domain name:&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;ol style="margin-left: 25px; direction: ltr; list-style-position: outside; text-align: justify;"&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;For purchasing the name we advise you to use the searching engines in order to select
            the appealing provider of the domains. You just need to enter “domain names” in
            the search field of for example Google. Please, make sure that you are the only
            owner of the website. If a provider offers to register the name with the third party,
            it means that the third party is able to use the ownership rights at any moment.
            After that you need to decide on the domain name. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The acquired domain must be available and not registered by anybody else. As a rule,
            providers offer a service of checking whether the domain is available or not. If
            not, then you can do that yourself and free of charge at &lt;a href="http://www.whois-service.com/"&gt;
                www.whois-service.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ol&gt;
    &lt;ol style="margin-left: 25px; direction: ltr; list-style-position: outside; text-align: justify;"
        start="3"&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The registered domain name must comply with the website theme. If you are buying
            a name not related to Forex and online trading, investments i.e., it will be difficult
            for you to optimize the site for searching engines. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The domain name must be maximally simple and easy to remember. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The free domains of the type “instaforex.wordpress.com” cannot be used for building
            a website.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;We would prefer you to buy the domain of the second level rather than of the third
            one. Thus, for example, the domain “wikipedia.org” is of the second level and “ru.wikipedia.org”
            is a third-level domain.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;A domain name should not coincide with or look similar to the word "&lt;b&gt;InstaForex&lt;/b&gt;", whatever the language it is written in is. Domain
            names not accepted for consideration are as follows: instaforex-****.com, instaforex.**,
            instaforex****.com, insta****.** ( *** means any words and word combinations). If
            you have any questions concerning the domain name you chose, please contact InstaForex Partnership Department by email: &lt;a href="mailto:partners@mail.instaforex.com"&gt;
                    partners@mail.instaforex.com&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ol&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;These are the main guidelines which will help you to acquire an appropriate domain
    name. Right after the domain has been registered, specify it in the application
    form for getting an absolutely toll-free partner website. Further instructions will
    be sent to the email address indicated in your application form for receiving a
    partner website.&lt;/p&gt;

  <data name="Hedging" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>Hedging</value>
  </data>
  <data name="NettingDesc" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>&lt;b&gt;Netting&lt;/b&gt; is a money-management system that implies that only one position can be opened on a given trading instrument at any one time.
If you have opened a position on a certain instrument and then opened one more trade in the same direction (buy/sell), then the value of the positions will be consolidated. If you start an opposite trade, the value of the open position will be reduced. If a new opposite position is equal in value, your existing position will be closed. In case the value of a new position exceeds that of the first trade, the latter will be reversed.
The system works for both pending and market orders.</value>

  <data name="CryptoInstructionInitialText" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>&lt;p&gt;When checking addresses on various Ethereum blockchain explorers, such as Etherscan, you may notice some addresses that have internal and external transactions as well as token transfers. To find out what is the difference between these operations, first we need to understand the concept of external and internal addresses in the Ethereum blockchain.&lt;/p&gt;</value>
  </data>
  <data name="CryptoInstructionAddressesText" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;External and internal addresses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Users can access external addresses through private keys, whereas internal addresses cannot be accessed directly unlike wallets. To use an internal address, one should call its functions.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Here is an example:&lt;br&gt;
&lt;img class="img-responsive" src="/img/crypto-instruction/image1.png" style="display: inline;"/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;This address has several entries in the Transactions tab: some of them are outgoing and some incoming. All these transactions are external because they were either sent to external accounts or received from them.&lt;/p&gt;</value>
  </data>
  <data name="CryptoInstructionTransactionTypesText" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;The Transactions tab shows all transactions initiated by external accounts regardless of who initiated them - whether a sender or a receiver.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;Now let’s have a look at the second tab of our first address: Internal Transactions.&lt;br&gt;
&lt;img class="img-responsive" src="/img/crypto-instruction/image4.png" style="display: inline;"/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;The Internal Transactions tab reflects all transactions that were initiated by internal accounts as a result of one or several preceding transactions.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;As seen on the screenshot above, there are three tabs, excluding the Comments, and the first two of them show Transactions and Internal Transactions. Those are referred to direct transfers and they are &lt;b&gt;available to InstaForex clients for depositing their accounts.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</value>
  </data>
  <data name="CryptoInstructionTokenTransfersText" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Token transfers&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;Finally, let’s pay attention to the Token Transfers tab.&lt;br&gt;
&lt;img class="img-responsive" src="/img/crypto-instruction/image6.png" style="display: inline;" /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;The name of this operation is self-explanatory. Token transfers are essentially transactions for transferring tokens. In the given example we can see the ERC20 token that has standardized functions. An entry about it will appear in this tab only if the transaction will be intended for transferring tokens. There is a great variety of tokens, and such transfers are not available to InstaForex clients.&lt;/p&gt;</value>
  </data>
  <data name="CryptoInstructionConclusionText" xml:space="preserve">
    <value>&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;To sum up&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Now you know how to distinguish various transactions in the Ethereum blockchain with the help of Etherscan. You can tell apart token transfers that are not available to InstaForex clients and direct transfers that can be used by them.&lt;/p&gt;</value>
  </data>
